< Text>
Beautiful - just like the pictures. Once you park, you can take a trail that is labeled "Garapatta Beach." I think the easiest way down (albeit a little longer) would be to take the stairs down to the beach, and then walk all the way right towards the stream of water joining the ocean. If you follow the stream up then you enter the valley.

Alternatively you take a right off the original fork in the park, which will take you on a path to the top of the valley. From here there are various ways to get down into the valley, albeit some are steep. Definitely a must see!<//Text>

<text>My visit in early March was rewarded with beautiful blooms.  Parking was easy and the Google map was spot on.   The trail length was only about a half mile putting you at a nice beach with sweeping views that are amazing.  The waves are dangerous, so be very careful because there is no place to run in high tide.  I was surprised at how many people were enjoying the trails, and how many of the lilies were trampled,  however it was still beautiful.< /text>< name>

<Review>I have been to this park many times.
I came back again on April/4/2021. Spring is the perfect time to be  visiting as the Calla Lillies and wildflowers are in full bloom.
Parked my car at  Gate 18 within Garrapata State Park and walked for 5 minutes down until I reached the set of stairs descending to the Calla Lilly Valley. The whole hike took me about half a mile roundtrip.
The Calla Lilly is such an elegant-looking flower and the epicenter of the valley's scenic bloom.
At any time of day, this place is beautiful‚Ä¶but the golden hour is at  sunset, as it is extra special then.
The phenomenon of scattering is also why the sky turns red, orange, and pink at sunset.
This is definitely one of the most picturesque coastal areas in Big Sur.<//Review>< time>
1617658612658< /time>

< Rate>
5< /Rate>
< text>
Gorgeous! This is an unmarked trailhead, you park along the highway. Pay close attention to Google maps as you approach the area and Google will take you right to the trailhead. You will likely see a few other cars parked on the side alerting you this is the location. Trailhead leads to stairs down into Calla Lilly Valley, less than five minute walk. You can also proceed another half mile down the road and park at the Garrupta State Beach sign, take the stairs to the beach, and then walk back along the beach to Calla Lilly Valley.<//text>

< review>
Came here for Mother's Day brunch, so this review is a bit overdue. When I had made the reservations, I did not realize that for Mother's Day brunch, their only service was buffet style and we were expected full table service. I looked at my confirmation and this was not indicated anywhere, but we made the most of it and we weren't disappointed.

This restaurant is located inside Marriott and we walked through their beautiful lobby to get to it. The restaurant is also very large, spacious, and with a few separate dining areas. It was a bit pricey.. But there was a wide variety of food options, fresh and high quality. My kids took full advantage of their waffles and unlimited Nutella. LoL. There was also seafood, an omelette station as well as a crepe station. Plenty of fresh fruit and bite size desserts as well.

Some parts of the restaurant had a lovely view of the marina. After brunch, we were able to sneak outside and take a stroll by the water and the hotel's lovely pool area while keeping our car with valet. This can be a little tricky though, because their doors require a hotel room key to return inside.. it was a busy Sunday afternoon, so we were just lucky we were able to go out and back in without trouble.< /review>

< userid>
105692744256480109238< /userid>
<user_name>Chelsea Madren (OC Food Diva)</user_name><date>1465487420634<//date><Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Burrata Cheese ($14) is served with tomato jam, speck, and toasted bread. The burrata is like a creamy cloud of cheese. It‚Äôs so soft and mild, it pairs well with the tomato jam and speck, adding both sweet and salty notes. The toasted bread is the perfect delivery vehicle for this starter. Rating: 5/5

Seafood Salad ($19) is Dungeness crab, rock shrimp, and Maine lobster atop gem lettuce and avocado green goddess dressing. It‚Äôs the perfect spring/summer salad to enjoy while overlooking the lush tropical pool area. The crab, shrimp, and lobster are cooked to perfection, each with their own unique flavor notes of sweet and briny flavors. The dressing has a nice flavor and lends itself nicely to the seafood, adding flavor without overpowering. Rating: 5/5

Brandt Beef Flat Iron ($26.50) is a grilled flat iron steak topped with herb butter and served with arugula salad and truffle fries. This has to be the best flat iron steak around! The steak has the tender texture of filet mignon but with subtle marbling. The knife cuts through like butter. The herb butter adds an herbal essence bringing out the sweetness of the beef. The truffle fries are so aromatic and highly addictive indeed; crispy on the outside and fluffy on the inside with truffle flavor and aroma in every bite. Rating: 5/5

Maker‚Äôs Mark Milkshake ($14) is served with maple lacquered pepper bacon. It has a creamy texture from the ice cream. The Maker‚Äôs Mark bourbon packs a punch but lends a caramel-like flavor to the shake. The added bacon shakes things up with a little bit of salty. This also won the ‚ÄúBest Dessert‚Äù at the San Diego Bay Food & Wine Festival. Rating: 5/5< /Review>

<Review>Came here for late lunch on a Sunday,

As of this date, they're still offering OUT DOOR dining. (2 tables outside)

I really enjoy that they have lunch specials 7 days a week! (Typically not on weekends)

Papaya salad: I asked for hot, and a bit sweeter than usual. Got a good kick, not for amateur spice eaters. Really fresh veggies.

Beef salad: medium, wish I got it in hot. (We wanted to see the difference b/n hot and medium). None the less, again, super fresh veggies and beef was cooked well. Would like to see more asian/aromatic veggies to enhance the dish.

Pad thai- Got the lunch special. Portion is decent for lunch. I was skeptical about how watery the sauce/texture was at first, but the flavor makes up for the doubt. Sauce eventually thickened and it was really good.

Service: really kind, and I appreciate that they wore masks and upheld the covid rules while still giving good service.

Will be back!< /Review>< username>
Jessica Thalia< /username>

< Text>
I drive all the way to AM Thai to get some lunch specials of Pad See Eww for $7.95 and 2 orders of Orange Chickens for my 4 yr old daughter.. cuz she loves this chicken!!

Either dining in or taking out, the Employees are always friendly and they make sure you are treated right.

During the weekdays, the lunch hours between 11:30am-2pm are not so busy, so if you are near by, make sure to visit AM to get your lunch specials.. FOR $7.95! it's really good stuff and right amount of flavor they make.

I ordered a Pad See Eww lunch special and 2 orders of regular orange chickens, and my order came out within 10 minutes.. and my to go orders were ready right before I was done with my food, packaged nicely in a plastic bag.

For Thai food near Anaheim, I can't find anywhere else than Am.
They have a relatively large parking lot, and they are right next to the Indian Cuisine.

Their restroom is clean and organized, and they can serve as many as 10+ people on their long tables inside.

Good food, good price, and friendly employees should never go wrong.
will be back for more Thai next month!</Text>

<Text>I love that there's a good Thai restaurant right next to my work! One of the main reasons why I come here is because of their lunch special. It's about 8 dollars and it's very delicious in flavors!

I decided to come for dinner with my girlfriend because we both crave thai food all the time! No joke. There's quite of few thai places in Buena Park, this one is actually one of the better ones.

< Text>
We discovered this place a few months ago and keep coming back. The service is excellent and the food comes out a few minutes after ordering. I drink a few glasses of water to tone down the heat.

Enjoy!<//Text>

< text>
This church is my community, and my family. I started coming here right after moving here from Seattle where we were going to another congregation. I thought we moved here for a job, but realized that it was to be a part of growing God's house and to be a part of the Coachella vision. That's a vision that really resonated with me. 1. Diverse: This is a place where you can belong before you believe. Members can invite their friends and everyone is welcome. The diversity is nice with people from all walks of life, ages, ethnicities and races coming together. A little glimpse of heaven.

Love the passion of this church for its house and the bay area. But you gotta come check it out for yourself.< /text>

This is the fifth medical cannabis dispensary in San Jose that I have been to. The people are really nice, and professional. They have a very clean place as well. This is quite possibly one of the most efficient and professional medical marijuana dispensaries I have ever been to.

I've recommended to 4 of my family members confidently because I know they will be treated well and experience a great sense of well being after coming here just like I did.</review>

I have been going to Amsterdam's Garden basically since their doors opened. Their location is easy to find and parking is never an issue. If you have checked out other places, you will soon find they really do have the best cannabis in San Jose. I have never had to wait more than 10 minutes to be seen.

They generally have 12+ varieties at a time and those varieties change on a weekly basis. The quality is top notch and the prices are fair based on that quality. They offer edibles, including pre-made goodies and a wide array of concentrates.

All in all, this dispensary has everything I need in a nice, friendly environment that is easily accessible. I highly recommend this dispensary for all those in the Bay Area.< /review>

<text>Being from Mountain View, I have only been to five or six cannabis clubs in San Jose but this one is my favorite so far. It's pretty quick and easy to reach, right off of 880 next to Santa Clara University.

The white mansion looks like a Greek building with the columns. The lobby is comfortable and doesn't make me feel like I'm in a warehouse or a pawn shop. I went in the "budroom" room which had 2 budtenders. I told him I didn't like to smoke a lot and he recommended some capsules and tinctures---very effective! I also picked up some kief, which he described as a "concentrate" so you don't have to smoke as much. They have first time patient gifts and discounts for bulk purchases.

My medicine (white widow) worked really well, and I was very happy with the information I got. I really appreciate the one on one privacy they offer. Will definitely come back here.<//text><Name>Isis Williams< /Name>< rate>
